        initScript(), t.currentTarget.removeEventListener(t.type, loadScriptOnEvent)
    }

    function initScript() {
        if (window.scriptInit) return !1;
        window.scriptInit = !0;
        var _i = document.createElement('script'),
            _s = document.scripts[0];
        _i.defer = true;
        _i.src = '//www.google.com/recaptcha/api.js?onload=vueRecaptchaApiLoaded&render=explicit';
        _s.parentNode.insertBefore(_i, _s);
    }

    function initScriptGSI() {
        if (window.scriptInitGSI) return !1;
        window.scriptInitGSI = !0;
        var _i = document.createElement('script'),
            _s = document.scripts[0];
        _i.defer = true;
        _i.src = 'https://accounts.google.com/gsi/client';
        _s.parentNode.insertBefore(_i, _s);
    }
